    <td style="padding-top:0.01in;vertical-align:top;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</span></p></td>
    <td style="padding-top:0.01in;vertical-align:top;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</span></p></td>
    <td style="padding-top:0.01in;vertical-align:top;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</span></p></td>
    <td style="padding-top:0.01in;vertical-align:top;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.3pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:4.3pt;text-align:left;"><span style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;min-width:fit-content;">Runway Growth Finance Corp.</span></p></td>
   </tr>

  <title>EX-99.1</title>
 </head>
 <body style="margin: auto!important;padding: 8px;">
  <div style="min-height:0.5in;"></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:14pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Runway Growth Finance Corp. Reports First Quarter 2024 Financial Results</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Delivered Total and Net Investment Income of $40.0 million and $18.7 million, Respectively</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Investment Portfolio of $1.0 billion</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Chairman, President and CEO David Spreng Returns from Medical Leave</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Conference Call Today, Tuesday, May 7, 2024 at 5:00 p.m. ET</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">MENLO PARK, Calif., May 7, 2024&#x2014;Runway Growth Finance Corp. (Nasdaq: RWAY) </font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">(&#x201c;Runway Growth&#x201d; or the &#x201c;Company&#x201d;),</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> a leading provider of flexible capital solutions to late- and growth-stage companies seeking an alternative to raising equity, today announced its financial results for the first quarter ended March 31, 2024. The Company also announced that David Spreng will resume his full responsibilities as Chairman, President and Chief Executive Officer of the Company, effective today, May 7, 2024.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:4pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">First Quarter 2024 Highlights</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Total investment income of $40.0 million </font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Net investment income of $18.7 million, or $0.46 per share</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Net asset value of $13.36 per share</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Dollar-weighted annualized yield on debt investments of 17.4% for the quarter</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Two investments completed in new and existing portfolio companies, representing $25.0 million in funded loans and other investments</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Aggregate proceeds of $34.4 million received from principal prepayments, and $0.4 million received from scheduled amortization</font></div></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:4pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Second Quarter 2024 Distributions</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:6pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Declared second quarter 2024 regular dividend of $0.40 per share</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:6pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Declared second quarter 2024 supplemental dividend of $0.07 per share </font></div></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#x201c;In the first quarter, Runway Growth delivered solid financial performance, generated increased pipeline activity, as well as enhanced revenue and lead generation opportunities through the establishment of our joint venture with Cadma Capital Partners,&#x201d; said David Spreng, Founder and CEO of Runway Growth. &#x201c;As the current venture ecosystem continues to evolve, we are employing prudent selectivity and underwriting rigor as we look to deploy our ample dry powder in the coming quarters. Maintaining and enhancing credit quality is our primary priority as we have continued confidence in our portfolio&#x2019;s earnings power and ability to provide consistent distributions to our shareholders. Looking ahead, our team will maintain this level of discipline as we seek to partner with best-in-class companies in the industries we know best, and deliver sustainable risk-adjusted returns for our shareholders.&#x201d;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">First Quarter 2024 Operating Results</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Total investment income for the quarter ended March 31, 2024 was $40.0 million, compared to $39.3 million for the quarter ended March 31, 2023.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Net investment income for the quarter ended March 31, 2024 was $18.7 million, or $0.46 per share, compared to $18.2 million, or $0.45 per share, for the quarter ended March 31, 2023.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Company's dollar-weighted annualized yield on average debt investments for the quarter ended March 31, 2024</font><font style="color:#231f20;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">,</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> was 17.4%</font><font style="color:#231f20;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">. </font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Company calculates the yield on dollar-weighted debt investments for any period measured as (1) total</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <div style="flex-direction:column;display:flex;min-height:0.5in;justify-content:flex-end;"></div>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <div style="min-height:0.5in;"></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">investment-related income during the period divided by (2) the daily average of the fair value of debt investments outstanding during the period.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Total operating expenses for the quarter ended March 31, 2024 were $21.3 million, compared to $21.1 million for the quarter ended March 31, 2023.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Net realized loss on investments was $0 for the quarter ended March 31, 2024, compared to a net realized loss of $1.2 million for the quarter ended March 31, 2023.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">For the quarter ended March 31, 2024, net change in unrealized loss on investments was $6.6 million, compared to a net change in unrealized loss on investments of $5.1 million for the comparable prior year period.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Portfolio and Investment Activity</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">As of March 31, 2024, Runway Growth&#x2019;s investment portfolio had an aggregate fair value of approximately $1.02 billion  in 53 portfolio companies, and was comprised of approximately $969.6 million in term loans, 98.5% of which are senior secured loans and $46.8 million in warrants and other equity-related investments.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">During the first quarter of 2024, Runway Growth completed two investments in new and existing portfolio companies, representing $24.6 million in funded loans, net of upfront loan origination fees.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Total portfolio investment activity for the three months ended March 31, 2024, and 2023 was as follows:</font></p>

    <td style="vertical-align:bottom;"><p style="font-size:8pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p></td>

    <td style="vertical-align:bottom;text-align:left;"><p style="font-size:8pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p></td>

    <td style="vertical-align:bottom;"><p style="font-size:8pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p></td>

  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Net Asset Value</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">As of March 31, 2024, net asset value (&#x201c;NAV&#x2019;&#x201d;) per share was $13.36, compared to $14.07 as of March 31, 2023. Total net assets at the end of the first quarter was $529.5 million, down 7% from $569.8 million in the quarter ended March 31, 2023.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">For the quarter ended March 31, 2024, net increase in net assets resulting from operations was $12.0 million, or $0.30 per share, compared to a net increase in net assets resulting from operations of $12.0 million, or $0.30 per share, for the quarter ended March 31, 2023.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Liquidity and Capital Resources</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">As of March 31, 2024, the Company had approximately $319.9 million in available liquidity, including unrestricted cash and cash equivalents of $6.9 million and $313.0 million in available borrowing capacity under the Company&#x2019;s credit facility, subject to existing terms, advance rates and regulatory and covenant requirements.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Company ended the quarter with a core leverage ratio of approximately 91%, compared to 95% for the quarter ended December 31, 2023.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>

  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Distributions</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">On April 30, 2024, the Company&#x2019;s board of directors declared a regular quarterly distribution of $0.40 per share for the second quarter of 2024, payable on May 24, 2024, to stockholders of record as of May 10, 2024. In addition, the Company&#x2019;s board of directors declared a supplemental distribution of $0.07 per share for the second quarter of 2024 that is also payable on May 24, 2024 to stockholders of record as of May 10, 2024.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Share Repurchase Program</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">On November 2, 2023, the Company&#x2019;s board of directors approved a share repurchase program (the &#x201c;Share Repurchase Program&#x201d;) under which the Company may repurchase up to $25.0 million of its outstanding common stock. Under the Share Repurchase Program, purchases may be made at management&#x2019;s discretion from time to time in open-market transactions, in accordance with all applicable securities laws and regulations.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Recent Developments</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Company evaluated events subsequent to </font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">March 31, 2024</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> through May 7, 2024, the date the consolidated financial statements were issued.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">On April 26, 2024 Echo360 Inc. prepaid its outstanding principal balance of $25.3 million on the Company's senior secured loan.</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">On April 30, 2024, the board of directors declared a regular quarterly distribution of $0.40 per share and a supplemental distribution of $0.07 per share for stockholders of record on May 10, 2024 payable on or before May 24, 2024</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">On April 30, 2024, following his return from temporary medical leave and upon the approval of the Company's board of directors, Mr. Spreng, was reinstated as the Company's President and Chief Executive Officer.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">For the period commencing March 31, 2024 through May 7, 2024, the Company repurchased 183,702 shares under the Share Repurchase Program.</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>

  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Conference Call</font></p>

  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">About Runway Growth Finance Corp.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Runway Growth is a growing specialty finance company focused on providing flexible capital solutions to late- and growth-stage companies seeking an alternative to raising equity. Runway Growth is a closed-end investment fund that has elected to be regulated as a business development company under the Investment Company Act of 1940, as amended. Runway Growth is externally managed by Runway Growth Capital LLC, an established registered investment advisor that was formed in 2015 and led by industry veteran David Spreng. For more information, please visit </font><font><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">www.runwaygrowth.com</font></font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></p>
